604:The brief requires every chip to resolve on `(run_id, event_id, produced_file_id, produced_version_id)`. The existing `iee_artifacts` table is keyed on `iee_run_id` (FK to `iee_runs.id`), not directly on `agent_runs.id`. The join path from agent run → artifact is `agent_runs.id → agent_runs.iee_run_id (= iee_runs.id) → iee_artifacts.iee_run_id`. We extend the table with:
607:ALTER TABLE iee_artifacts
608:  ADD COLUMN agent_run_id UUID REFERENCES agent_runs(id),               -- denormalised for lineage queries; populated at write time
610:  ADD COLUMN produced_version_id UUID;                                   -- stable version handle; allocated at write time
612:CREATE INDEX iee_artifacts_agent_run_idx ON iee_artifacts (agent_run_id) WHERE agent_run_id IS NOT NULL;
613:CREATE INDEX iee_artifacts_event_idx     ON iee_artifacts (producing_event_id) WHERE producing_event_id IS NOT NULL;
614:CREATE INDEX iee_artifacts_version_idx   ON iee_artifacts (produced_version_id) WHERE produced_version_id IS NOT NULL;
619:`produced_version_id` is allocated at the moment the artifact is written; subsequent re-writes of the same logical filename produce a *new* row with a new `produced_version_id`. Every chip is keyed on the four-tuple; clicks resolve to the exact version produced at that event.
621:**Backfill:** `agent_run_id` is nullable for legacy rows. New writes set it; existing rows stay null. Phase 5 chips render only for events whose `iee_artifacts` rows have all four fields populated; legacy rows surface as un-chipped events with no degradation in the surrounding UI.
623:### 6.6 `users.default_agent_tab` (Phase 2, migration 0289)
626:ALTER TABLE users
627:  ADD COLUMN default_agent_tab TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'overview'
628:    CHECK (default_agent_tab IN ('overview','configure','behaviour','personality','skills','scorecards','data-sources','schedule','budget','runs'));
631:Per-user preference; the AgentEditPage reads it on mount. No feature flag. New column only; no backfill required (`DEFAULT 'overview'` covers existing rows).
637:| Run lifecycle events (canonical) | `agent_execution_events` | Indefinite | None — immutable. |
638:| Typed observations | `agent_observations` | 90 days default; `is_pinned = TRUE` indefinite | `agentObservationsPruneJob` daily. |
640:| Current focus snapshots | In-memory (Redis or equivalent) | Ephemeral, session-bound | TTL 60s on each cache write. Never persisted. |
641:| Activity feed projection | `agent_execution_events` filtered | 60 days visible; older paged via `View all` from canonical | No projection table; activity feed reads canonical with limit + cursor. |
645:Pruning a projection MUST NOT invalidate any user-visible surface; if Overview surfaces data older than the retention window, the surface fails closed (shows *"older than X days, view in Run trace"*) rather than rendering stale data.
672:1. failed              — agent is in terminal error state (canonical terminal event present)
673:2. degraded            — any §12.3 degradation condition is currently true AND no terminal event present
677:6. scheduled           — no active run, next run time is known
678:7. idle                — none of the above
681:`failed` ranks above `degraded` because telemetry staleness must never mask a canonical terminal failure. If the run has emitted a terminal failure event, the resolver returns `failed` regardless of the freshness of subsequent telemetry. `degraded` is only entered when the run is still in flight per the canonical event log AND telemetry has gone stale.
683:**Producer:** `agentPresenceService.resolveAgentPresence(agentId, ctx)` writes to `agent_presence_projections` on every `agent_execution_events` tail-event for that agent.
684:**Consumers:** every presence-aware UI surface (Overview hero pill, Home Active Agents widget, sidebar agent list, run trace header, activity badges, Inbox notifications) reads from this projection. UI MUST NOT re-derive state from raw signals (brief §5.3).
688:### 7.2 `CurrentFocus`
694:export interface CurrentFocus {

711:1. `agent_runs.current_step_summary` of the active run (latest non-idle step).

717:**Anti-fake-progress validator** (brief §5.1 hard rule): the focus-line summariser rejects copy that lacks at least one of (a) a concrete step number, (b) a concrete entity / object id or name, or (c) a concrete blocking condition. Forbidden patterns: `*Thinking*`, `*Analysing data*`, `*Working on task*`, `*Reasoning about*`, `*Preparing*`, `*Processing*`, any `-ing` verb without an object. If the latest event has no concrete subject, the focus line falls back to the explicit stale-state copy rather than synthesising filler.
720:**Consumer:** Overview tab `PresenceHero` + Home widget rows.
733:**Append-only invariant:** there is no `UPDATE` path. Corrections create a new row with `supersedes_observation_id` set. The Overview surface reads the latest non-superseded row in each thread; the run trace and audit views show the full history.
757:**Consumer:** Overview tab (`RecentObservationsCard`) reads top-N `WHERE supersedes_observation_id IS NULL` ordered by `created_at DESC`.

801:- `GET /api/agents/:id/files-snapshot?limit=...&cursor=...` — beyond initial 3.

Run-trace lineage chips reference the four-tuple only.
810:**Worst-case profiling:** spec author MUST profile the *50-runs-today, 200-pinned-observations, 30-knowledge-entries-loaded* worst case before declaring layout shippable. The 150KB target holds at the 95th-percentile worst case; design for graceful degradation (more aggressive lazy-loading) above it rather than blowing the budget.
812:**PR-review check.** Every new Overview surface added later asserts a payload-impact note in its PR. The §13.7 freshness matrix and §7.4 budget are paired contracts: every new surface picks one row in each.
816:**Definition:** Working Time is the sum of intervals during which an `agent_execution_events.step_started` event has fired and a matching `step_completed` event has not yet fired, for runs owned by this agent — **minus** any nested intervals where the worker is in a declared wait state (HITL pause, external dependency wait, retry backoff). The accounting boundary is *worker-side compute*: the run engine and the IEE worker emit explicit start/end events when entering and exiting wait states; Working Time accumulates only outside those wait windows.
820:| Pair | Accumulates? | Notes |
825:| `hitl_pause_started` → `hitl_pause_resolved` | **Subtracted** | Operator-blocked. |
833:| Active LLM call or worker-local tool call (state = `running`, no nested wait state) | Yes | Yes |
834:| Queue wait before a step starts | No | No |
835:| HITL pause (state = `waiting_on_human`) | No | No |
836:| External API in flight (state = `waiting_on_dependency`, between `external_call_started` and `external_call_completed`) | No | No |
837:| Retry backoff between attempts | No | No |
838:| Sub-agent delegation | Yes for parent (only for non-delegated portions) and Yes for sub-agent (both attributed separately; rolls up to parent run for invoice) | Yes for both |
840:| Concurrent runs of the same agent | Time intervals **summed, not deduplicated** | Yes |
841:| Time spent in `degraded` state | Best-effort included based on last known step timestamps; if the step envelope never closed, accumulate up to the last observed event and stop | Yes |

Tested via pure unit. Per-agent charts and per-agent invoice lines reconcile 1:1.

941:**Cross-cutting rule:** surfaces driven by SSE share **one connection per Overview tab** and one connection per Home widget. No three-independent-channels pattern.
943:**Idempotency check:** `agent_presence_projections` upserts use `INSERT … ON CONFLICT (agent_id) DO UPDATE` with the §11.1 watermark predicate (per-run `(last_event_run_id, last_event_run_seq)` plus cross-run server-side `last_event_timestamp` tiebreaker). The watermark composes per-run + cross-run because `agent_execution_events.sequence_number` is run-scoped, not global; replayed events never overwrite newer state (brief §5.2 *no rollback by replay*).

951:Forward-only. No phase references a primitive introduced in a later phase.

970:Per spec-authoring checklist Section 10, every new write path declares idempotency / retry / concurrency / terminal events.
976:| `INSERT INTO agent_observations` | `key-based` | `UNIQUE (idempotency_key)` — duplicate observation emit for the same logical observation is rejected. The key is computed by the writer from `(event_id, source_id, observation_type, normalised_body_hash)` so multiple distinct observations of the same type from the same event are permitted. `(supersedes_observation_id)` is allowed many-to-one (multiple corrections superseding the same root). |
978:| `UPSERT agent_presence_projections` | `state-based` | Predicate: accept if `(excluded.last_event_run_id = projections.last_event_run_id AND excluded.last_event_run_seq > projections.last_event_run_seq) OR excluded.last_event_timestamp > projections.last_event_timestamp`. Per-run sequence is the within-run watermark; cross-run uses server-side monotonic timestamp from `agent_execution_events.event_timestamp`. |
979:| `INSERT INTO agent_working_time_rollups` (upsert) | `key-based` | The ledger is the single mechanism. `agent_working_time_event_ledger.event_id` is the PK; the writer inserts into the ledger first (`INSERT INTO ledger ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING RETURNING event_id`); only on a non-empty RETURNING does it apply the contribution to the rollup bucket(s) in the same transaction. Replays, retries, and out-of-order events are all idempotent. The rollup table has no sequence watermark of its own; idempotency lives at the per-event ledger. |
980:| `INSERT INTO iee_artifacts` (with `producing_event_id`, `produced_version_id`) | `key-based` | `produced_version_id` is allocated at write time; subsequent re-writes of the same logical filename produce a new row with a new version id. No upsert path — every write is a new row. |
981:| Session heartbeat update | `safe` (state-based) | `UPDATE … WHERE id = $1 AND status IN ('active','idle')` — heartbeat after teardown is a no-op (0 rows updated). |
988:| Observation append | `guarded` | UNIQUE on `idempotency_key` (computed by writer from `(event_id, source_id, observation_type, normalised_body_hash)`) |
992:| Heartbeat | `safe` | Idempotent; 0-rows-updated path is no-op |
994:| Stream reconnect with `Last-Event-ID` | `safe` | Server filters events on `(event_timestamp, event_id) > (lastSeen)`; older events are recorded for audit but not re-applied to live projection |
1000:| Two parallel runs of same agent (concurrent scheduled triggers) | Two distinct `iee_sessions` rows — `UNIQUE (run_id)` permits this. Working-time intervals **sum, not deduplicate** (brief §5.4). | n/a — both win |
1001:| Two writers attempting to create a session for the same run | `UNIQUE (run_id)` → 23505 → mapped to HTTP 409 with error body referencing the existing session id | 409 with `{ existingSessionId: ... }` |
1003:| Two clients both attempting to set the user's default tab simultaneously (v1.1 only — no v1 write path) | Last-write-wins (`users.default_agent_tab` is a single column) | 200 with the persisted value |
1004:| Replay storm (event stream reconnect) | Sequence-watermark on `agent_presence_projections.(last_event_run_id, last_event_run_seq)` + cross-run timestamp tiebreaker; `agent_working_time_event_ledger` makes per-event folding key-based and idempotent — older replayed events ignored | n/a — silently skipped, audit logged |
1011:| Run lifecycle (existing) | `run_completed` (existing) | `success | partial | failed` | No new events with same `run_id` after terminal — existing contract |
1012:| Session lifecycle | Session row's `released_at` set | `release_reason` ∈ closed enum | No further state transitions; `torn_down → *` forbidden |
1013:| Observation thread | Latest non-superseded row | n/a (each row is its own truth) | A superseded row never re-emerges as canonical |
1015:**No-silent-partial-success rule.** Run terminal events that complete with partial side-effects emit `status = 'partial'`. The Overview Working Time chart accounts the run as `partial_runs += 1`; the Working Time bar is coloured indigo (success portion) with red overlay (failed portion) per the brief §5 caption rule.
1023:| `users.default_agent_tab` (v1.1 only — no v1 write path) | 200 (idempotent — the value is what was set) | n/a |
1024:| `iee_artifacts UNIQUE` (existing) | n/a — every write produces a new row with a new `produced_version_id`; no upsert path | n/a |
1026:No 23505 ever bubbles as 500. Mapping enforced inside the service writer, not at the route boundary.
1030:Pure-function unit test: `accumulateWorkingTime(events)` for the closed-table cases in §7.5 and the brief §5.4. The reconciliation invariant — chart total equals invoice total — is asserted at the test level by computing both from the same `agent_working_time_rollups` rows and asserting equality. If a future invoice surface diverges (e.g. introduces its own rollup), this invariant must hold at the call-site or be explicitly broken with a recorded ADR.
1034:The freshness thresholds form one closed set, declared as constants in `shared/types/agentPresence.ts` and used by both the projection writer and the pure tests:
1047:`Current focus` displays MUST be wrapped in a freshness check at the resolver level: if the latest event's age exceeds `EVENT_STREAM_DELAYED` (10s) while status = `running`, the projection writer transitions `presence_state` to `degraded` with `degraded_reason = 'event_stream_delayed'` (per §12.3). The focus line is replaced with the §5.1 stale-state copy when the age exceeds `FOCUS_LINE_STALE_COPY` (30s). Both thresholds are enforced at projection-write time, not at the client.
1049:`failed` is reserved for terminal failure events emitted by the run engine — never inferred from telemetry silence. If the run truly completed while telemetry was stale, the next received event resolves `degraded` to `idle` per §12.3 *State on resolution*. If the run is genuinely stuck (no terminal event ever arrives), the agent stays in `degraded` until the worker heartbeat times out, at which point the orphan-cleanup path (Phase 4) writes a terminal failure event and the projection transitions to `failed` via the canonical chain.
1057:Seven values: `idle | running | waiting_on_human | waiting_on_dependency | scheduled | degraded | failed`. Adding a new value requires a spec amendment (§7.1 enforcement). The Postgres `CHECK` constraint on `agent_presence_projections.presence_state` is the database-level enforcement; the TypeScript discriminated union is the application-level enforcement.
1077:degraded → <freshly resolved primary state> (per §12.3 — resolver re-runs the §7.1 chain; NOT a return to the pre-degradation state)
1078:failed → idle (operator acknowledges; manual recovery)
1081:**Forbidden:** any transition not listed. `failed → running` directly is forbidden — the agent must transition through `idle` (operator-acknowledged recovery). Forbidden transitions are caught at the projection-writer layer; the writer rejects an upsert that would produce an illegal transition and logs `presence.illegal_transition_attempt` for audit.
1089:| `event_stream_delayed` | Server detects no new event from this run for 10s while activity is expected | Subtitle: "Presence delayed…" |
1090:| `worker_heartbeat_stale` | The IEE worker handling this run has not pinged in 30s | Subtitle: "Status uncertain" |
1091:| `focus_source_unavailable` | The latest event has no summarisable content | "(focus snapshot, X seconds ago)" |
1093:These three **server-observed** conditions are the only ones that populate `agent_presence_projections.degraded_reason`; the table's CHECK constraint pins the closed list. Each is detected on the server and is shared truth across all surfaces.
1095:**Client-side transport failures are NOT canonical presence.** When the client's SSE connection drops (network blip, tab paused, load-balancer flap), the client renders a **local** banner ("Reconnecting…") and freezes its tickers. The server-side `agent_presence_projections.presence_state` is unchanged — every other surface viewing the same agent continues to see the live state. Local transport health and canonical presence are two separate signals; conflating them lets one tab's disconnect mutate global state, which violates the brief §5.3 single-source-of-truth invariant. This separation is hard.
1097:**Recovery threshold.** `degraded` clears only after **two consecutive healthy heartbeat intervals** observed by the server-side projection writer. Recovery is entirely server-observed. Client-side resync acknowledgements (when an SSE client reconnects with `Last-Event-ID`) are a separate non-canonical signal that affects only that client's local UI; they do NOT mutate `agent_presence_projections.presence_state` (per the §12.3 client-vs-canonical separation).
1099:**Hysteresis window.** Minimum **10 seconds** in `degraded` before transitioning back. Prevents one-packet flicker. Implemented at the projection writer — the writer rejects a `degraded → primary` upsert if `NOW() - degraded_entered_at < INTERVAL '10 seconds'`.
1101:**Anti-oscillation rule.** If `degraded → healthy → degraded` happens twice within a 30-second window, the agent stays in `degraded` for the full 60-second hysteresis period regardless of subsequent healthy heartbeats. `degraded_oscillation_count` field on `agent_presence_projections` tracks within-window count; reset by the projection writer when the 30-second window elapses without an oscillation.
1103:**State on resolution.** Transitions to whatever the primary state actually is — derived fresh from the §7.1 resolution chain — not back to whatever it was before the degradation began. If the agent finished its run while telemetry was degraded, the resolved state is `idle`, not the prior `running`.
1108:- Duplicate events (same `event_id`) detected and ignored on second arrival.
1109:- **Older replayed events never overwrite newer resolved state.** If a replayed event's `event_timestamp = T1` arrives after the projection has advanced past `T2 > T1`, the event is recorded for audit but is NOT re-applied to the live presence projection.
1121:- Simpler reconnect semantics (`Last-Event-ID` header is built in).
1122:- Read-only event push fits the use case (the Overview tab does not push state to the server).
1123:- Lower complexity than WebSocket — no protocol upgrade negotiation.
1125:If a future surface ever needs a bidirectional channel, that surface adopts WebSocket independently — it does not retrofit onto this presence stream. The contract is SSE-only.
1129:- `GET /api/agent-presence/stream/:agentId` — per-agent stream, used by Overview tab.
1140:data: { agentId, presenceState, presenceSubtitle, lastEventId, lastEventTimestamp, serverNow }
1143:event: current_focus_updated
1144:data: { agentId, focus: CurrentFocus }
1160:data: { serverNow, lastEventId }    # sent every 15s; client uses to detect channel staleness
1165:- The browser's native `EventSource` automatically sends `Last-Event-ID: <last-seen-id>` as a header on reconnect once the connection has emitted at least one `id:` line. **Initial-open** does not carry a header. To resume after a deliberate close (e.g. tab restored from background), the client passes a `lastEventId` query parameter (`GET /api/agent-presence/stream/:agentId?lastEventId=<uuid>`) on initial open; the server prefers the query param, falls back to the header, and falls back to "no resume" if neither is present.
1166:- Server responds with all events since that id, in `(event_timestamp, event_id)` order, then resumes live.
1167:- If the client has been gone for longer than the server-side buffer (default 60s), the server sends a `presence_state_changed` event for the current canonical state (the client snaps to it) — no incremental replay. The buffer-overflow path is logged so operators can detect chronic flapping.
1168:- §12.4 replay semantics apply to the client-side projection: duplicates ignored, older events never overwrite newer resolved state, out-of-order within a batch sorted before applying.
1172:- Every event over the channel carries `serverNow` and `eventTimestamp` (server-side, monotonic from `agent_execution_events`).
1173:- Client elapsed-time tickers compute `now_server - event_timestamp_server` from server values, NOT from `Date.now()`.
1175:- The §13.7 freshness budgets are measured **server-to-client**, not by client measuring against its own clock.
1179:- **Single, server-confirmed snapshot per render.** No intermediate predictions leak into the UI.
1180:- **Allowed local synthesis** (presentation only): animating elapsed-time counter between server updates (the *0:42 elapsed* tick is fine; underlying timestamp is server-derived); smoothing the chart bar containing "now" between aggregation pushes; local hover/focus/expand UI state.
1181:- **Forbidden synthesis** (state simulation): pre-committing presence transitions; speculative `waiting_on_human` / `failed` / `degraded` / `completed` assertions; appending observations or knowledge-in-use entries without the server event; inventing activity-feed rows; "Run started" / "Run completed" surfacing before the server-side run-lifecycle event lands.
1182:- The hook MUST expose only the most recent server-confirmed snapshot. Optimistic update libraries (e.g. React Query's `optimisticData`) MUST NOT be used for presence state.
1188:| Status pill | <5s | SSE (no polling fallback — channel is locked SSE-only per §13.1) |
1189:| Current focus | <5s | SSE |
1193:| Knowledge in use | <5s active; last-run snapshot | SSE; snapshot persists between runs |
1194:| Files snapshot | <60s | Cached read; refresh on run-end |
1198:| Identity | Static | Read on tab mount |
1206:- **Reduced-motion.** Every animation honours `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce`. Pulse, fade, slide, marquee all gated. Reduced-motion users see static dots, instant pill transitions, no slide-in feed rows.
1207:- **ARIA live regions.** Status-pill changes, focus updates, activity-feed appends announced via `aria-live="polite"`; `waiting_on_human` and `failed` transitions use `aria-live="assertive"`.
1208:- **Screen-reader throttling.** Live updates rate-limited to **one announcement per 5s per surface**; high-activity bursts collapse to *"Outreach Agent: 12 new activity rows in the last minute"*, not 12 separate announcements.
1209:- **Layout stability.** Status pill width fixed across all 7 states. Activity feed appends below; existing rows do not reflow. Pre-rendered final-state heights for surfaces that update in place.

1250:### 15.1 Phase 1 (auto-knowledge-retrieval) — what we consume
1252:Owned by `tasks/builds/auto-knowledge-retrieval/` (separate branch). This spec consumes:
1256:| Knowledge → Files tab, filterable by agent | Cloud-compute deep-links from Overview Files snapshot card and Run trace lineage chips |
1257:| `retrieval.summary` events on `agent_execution_events` | Cloud-compute Knowledge-in-use card consumes the same data |
1258:| `reference_document_data_sources` table | Cloud-compute reads only; never writes |
1259:| `knowledge.files.deep_link` URL contract | Locked: `?agentId=...&runId=...&eventId=...&fileId=...&versionId=...` (extends Phase 1's likely shape with `runId/eventId/versionId`; Phase 1 must accept and resolve these query params) |
1265:| Overview Files snapshot card (Phase 2) | No | Reads raw `iee_artifacts` directly; surfaces filename + size + produced-at; no relevance signal; deep-link goes to a placeholder page until Phase 1 lands. |

### 6.6 `users.default_agent_tab` (Phase 2, migration 0289)

```sql
ALTER TABLE users
  ADD COLUMN default_agent_tab TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'overview'
```

### 6.7 Retention policy (per brief ¶õ5.7)

| Class | Source | Retention | Pruning job |
|---|---|---|---|
| Run lifecycle events (canonical) | `agent_execution_events` | Indefinite | None ƒ?" immutable. |
| Typed observations | `agent_observations` | 90 days default; `is_pinned = TRUE` indefinite | `agentObservationsPruneJob` daily. |
| Retrieval summaries | `retrieval.summary` events | Owned by Phase 1 ƒ?" 30 days at full fidelity | Phase 1 owns. |
| Current focus snapshots | In-memory (Redis or equivalent) | Ephemeral, session-bound | TTL 60s on each cache write. Never persisted. |
| Activity feed projection | `agent_execution_events` filtered | 60 days visible; older paged via `View all` from canonical | No projection table; activity feed reads canonical with limit + cursor. |
| Session summaries | `iee_sessions.summary` | 90 days | `ieeSessionsCompactJob` daily ƒ?" compacts blobs older than 90d, retains row. |
| Working Time aggregates | `agent_working_time_rollups` | 1 year per-day; older months collapse to monthly resolution | `workingTimeRollupCompactJob` monthly. |

Pruning a projection MUST NOT invalidate any user-visible surface; if Overview surfaces data older than the retention window, the surface fails closed (shows *"older than X days, view in Run trace"*) rather than rendering stale data.

---

## 7. Contracts

### 7.1 `AgentPresenceState` (closed enum)

**Type:** TypeScript discriminated union + Postgres `CHECK` constraint.

**Definition:**
```typescript
export const AGENT_PRESENCE_STATES = [
  'idle',
  'running',
  'waiting_on_human',
  'waiting_on_dependency',
  'scheduled',
  'degraded',
  'failed',
] as const;
export type AgentPresenceState = (typeof AGENT_PRESENCE_STATES)[number];
```

**Resolution order** (server-side, single resolver `resolveAgentPresence(agentId, ctx)`; first match wins; brief ¶õ5.3):

```
1. failed              ƒ?" agent is in terminal error state (canonical terminal event present)
2. degraded            ƒ?" any ¶õ12.3 degradation condition is currently true AND no terminal event present
3. waiting_on_human    ƒ?" active run is paused at a HITL gate
4. running             ƒ?" active run has at least one step in flight
5. waiting_on_dependency ƒ?" active run is paused on external system / lock / retry / sub-agent
6. scheduled           ƒ?" no active run, next run time is known
7. idle                ƒ?" none of the above
```

`failed` ranks above `degraded` because telemetry staleness must never mask a canonical terminal failure. If the run has emitted a terminal failure event, the resolver returns `failed` regardless of the freshness of subsequent telemetry. `degraded` is only entered when the run is still in flight per the canonical event log AND telemetry has gone stale.

**Producer:** `agentPresenceService.resolveAgentPresence(agentId, ctx)` writes to `agent_presence_projections` on every `agent_execution_events` tail-event for that agent.
**Consumers:** every presence-aware UI surface (Overview hero pill, Home Active Agents widget, sidebar agent list, run trace header, activity badges, Inbox notifications) reads from this projection. UI MUST NOT re-derive state from raw signals (brief ¶õ5.3).

**Adding a new state requires a spec amendment** (closed enum). The Postgres `CHECK` constraint is the enforcement mechanism.

### 7.2 `CurrentFocus`

**Type:** TypeScript object.

**Definition:**
```typescript
export interface CurrentFocus {
  text: string;                       // 140 chars max; one sentence
  truncated: boolean;
  fullText: string;                   // surfaced in tooltip on hover
  sourceEventId: string | null;       // anchors to agent_execution_events.id when sourced from a step
  sourceKind:                         // closed enum
    | 'active_run_step'
    | 'pending_hitl_gate'
    | 'scheduled_next_run'
    | 'last_completed_run'
    | 'static_fallback';
  serverNow: string;                  // ISO timestamp; client uses for elapsed-time math
  ageMs: number;                      // `serverNow - sourceEventTimestamp` (server-computed)
}
```

**Resolution chain** (first match wins; brief ¶õ5.3):
1. `agent_runs.current_step_summary` of the active run (latest non-idle step).
2. `pending_hitl_gate` description, when status = `waiting_on_human`.
3. `scheduled_next_run` description, when status = `scheduled`.
4. `last_completed_run.summary`, when status = `idle`.
5. Static fallback per brief ¶õ5.1 stale-state copy ("No recent activity (last event 4m ago)" with the actual age).

**Anti-fake-progress validator** (brief ¶õ5.1 hard rule): the focus-line summariser rejects copy that lacks at least one of (a) a concrete step number, (b) a concrete entity / object id or name, or (c) a concrete blocking condition. Forbidden patterns: `*Thinking*`, `*Analysing data*`, `*Working on task*`, `*Reasoning about*`, `*Preparing*`, `*Processing*`, any `-ing` verb without an object. If the latest event has no concrete subject, the focus line falls back to the explicit stale-state copy rather than synthesising filler.

**Producer:** `agentPresenceService` (server-side, runs at projection-update time).
**Consumer:** Overview tab `PresenceHero` + Home widget rows.

Truncation: 140 characters before middle-ellipsis on desktop; tighter on narrower viewports per existing responsive pattern.

### 7.3 `AgentObservation`

**Type:** Drizzle row + JSONB metadata.

**Required fields:**
- `id`, `agent_id`, `event_id`, `observation_type` (closed enum), `body`, `created_at`.

**Provenance invariant:** every row has `event_id` set. `event_id` references `agent_execution_events.id` for run-derived observations (`learned`, `detected`, `decided`, `flagged`, `produced`). The row's `metadata.source_kind` field discriminates the origin (closed enum: `run_step | retrieval_summary | tool_result | memory_block_insert`); the `metadata.source_id` field carries the underlying entity id (e.g. `agent_execution_events.id`, retrieval-summary event id, structured tool result id, `memory_blocks.id`).

**Append-only invariant:** there is no `UPDATE` path. Corrections create a new row with `supersedes_observation_id` set. The Overview surface reads the latest non-superseded row in each thread; the run trace and audit views show the full history.

**Example instance:**
```json
{
  "id": "f4ab...",
  "organisation_id": "00...",
  "agent_id": "ag1...",
  "run_id": "run...",
  "event_id": "evt...",
  "observation_type": "learned",
  "body": "Acme Corp has 12 directors with average tenure 3.4 years",
  "metadata": {
    "source_kind": "run_step",
    "source_id": "evt...",
    "summarised_from_step_seq": 7
  },
  "supersedes_observation_id": null,
  "is_pinned": false,
  "created_at": "2026-05-08T14:23:11Z"
}
```

**Producer:** `agentObservationService.append(...)` invoked from the run-step terminal-event hook in `agentExecutionService` and from the retrieval-summary handler.
**Consumer:** Overview tab (`RecentObservationsCard`) reads top-N `WHERE supersedes_observation_id IS NULL` ordered by `created_at DESC`.

### 7.4 `/api/agents/:id/overview` (initial payload contract)

**Type:** REST endpoint, JSON response.

**Response shape (initial payload, ƒ%Ï150KB compressed; brief ¶õ5.8):**
```json
{
  "identity": { "id": "...", "name": "...", "role": "...", "reportsTo": "...", "subaccountId": "..." },
  "presence": {
    "state": "running",
    "subtitle": null,
    "activeRunId": "run...",
    "currentFocus": { /* CurrentFocus */ },
    "elapsedSinceRunStartMs": 14211,
    "serverNow": "2026-05-08T14:23:11Z"
  },
  "activeGoals": [ { "type": "scheduled_run", "label": "Weekly Acme outreach", "nextRunAt": "..." } ],
  "recentObservations": [ /* top 3 typed observations; full payload for top 3 only */ ],
  "knowledgeInUse": [ /* top 3 entries with metadata; rest fetched on demand */ ],
  "filesSnapshot": [ /* top 3 files; deep-link to Phase 1 Knowledge ƒÅ' Files */ ],
  "toolsUsageBands": {
    "frequently": ["..."],
    "occasionally": ["..."],
    "rarely": ["..."],
    "asOf": "2026-05-08T13:00:00Z"
  },
  "schedulePeek": { "nextRunAt": "...", "trigger": "weekly_cron", "label": "Weekly Acme outreach" },
  "connectionsHealth": [ { "id": "...", "name": "...", "status": "healthy" } ],
  "workingTime": {
    "range": "today",
    "buckets": [ /* per-hour or per-day buckets with caption-bound rollup */ ],
    "captionTotalSeconds": 0,
    "captionRunsCount": 0,
    "captionSuccessRate": 0,
    "captionAverageRunDurationSeconds": 0
  },
  "activityFeed": [ /* first 5 rows; subsequent fetched on scroll or View all */ ]
}
```

**Lazy-load delegations** (brief ¶õ5.8 budget):
- `GET /api/agents/:id/observations?limit=...&cursor=...&pinned_only=...` ƒ?" beyond initial 3.
- `GET /api/agents/:id/files-snapshot?limit=...&cursor=...` ƒ?" beyond initial 3.
- `GET /api/agents/:id/tools-usage` ƒ?" beyond initial bands.
- `GET /api/agents/:id/activity-feed?limit=...&cursor=...` ƒ?" beyond initial 5.
- `GET /api/agents/:id/connections-health/:connectionId` ƒ?" per-connection diagnostic detail.
- `GET /api/agents/:id/working-time?range=week|month|quarter` ƒ?" non-active timeframes.
- `GET /api/agents/:id/knowledge-in-use/:entryId/provenance` ƒ?" full provenance panel.

**Inline-content prohibition** (brief ¶õ5.8): activity-feed rows reference `event_id` only; full event content fetched on click. Recent-observation rows beyond the initial 3 reference `observation_id` only. Knowledge-in-use entries hold metadata + source-document id; never embed source text inline. Run-trace lineage chips reference the four-tuple only.

**Worst-case profiling:** spec author MUST profile the *50-runs-today, 200-pinned-observations, 30-knowledge-entries-loaded* worst case before declaring layout shippable. The 150KB target holds at the 95th-percentile worst case; design for graceful degradation (more aggressive lazy-loading) above it rather than blowing the budget.

**PR-review check.** Every new Overview surface added later asserts a payload-impact note in its PR. The ¶õ13.7 freshness matrix and ¶õ7.4 budget are paired contracts: every new surface picks one row in each.

### 7.5 Working Time accounting (formal definition; brief ¶õ5.4)

**Definition:** Working Time is the sum of intervals during which an `agent_execution_events.step_started` event has fired and a matching `step_completed` event has not yet fired, for runs owned by this agent ƒ?" **minus** any nested intervals where the worker is in a declared wait state (HITL pause, external dependency wait, retry backoff). The accounting boundary is *worker-side compute*: the run engine and the IEE worker emit explicit start/end events when entering and exiting wait states; Working Time accumulates only outside those wait windows.

**Event pairs that bracket Working Time intervals:**

| Pair | Accumulates? | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| `step_started` ƒÅ' `step_completed` | Yes (as the outer envelope) | The matched envelope is required; an unmatched `step_started` falls into the `degraded` best-effort path below. |
| `tool_call_started` ƒÅ' `tool_call_completed` (worker-local tool, e.g. JSON transform, in-process LLM call) | Yes | Subset of the step interval; counts as Working Time. |
| `external_call_started` ƒÅ' `external_call_completed` (external API in flight, network round-trip) | **Subtracted** from the step interval | The worker is waiting; external service is doing the work. Subtraction is the mechanical rule. |
| `hitl_pause_started` ƒÅ' `hitl_pause_resolved` | **Subtracted** | Operator-blocked. |
| `retry_backoff_started` ƒÅ' `retry_backoff_completed` | **Subtracted** | Worker is sleeping. |
| `sub_agent_delegated` ƒÅ' `sub_agent_returned` | **Subtracted** for the parent (the parent's worker is awaiting the sub-agent); the sub-agent has its own `step_started` / `step_completed` envelope which counts as the sub-agent's Working Time. | Both agents bill separately; invoice rolls up. |

**Inclusion / exclusion summary:**

| Condition | Included? | Billed? |
|---|---|---|
| Active LLM call or worker-local tool call (state = `running`, no nested wait state) | Yes | Yes |
| Queue wait before a step starts | No | No |
| HITL pause (state = `waiting_on_human`) | No | No |
| External API in flight (state = `waiting_on_dependency`, between `external_call_started` and `external_call_completed`) | No | No |
| Retry backoff between attempts | No | No |
| Sub-agent delegation | Yes for parent (only for non-delegated portions) and Yes for sub-agent (both attributed separately; rolls up to parent run for invoice) | Yes for both |
| Failed step | Yes (up to failure timestamp; subtracts any nested wait windows that closed before failure) | Yes |
| Concurrent runs of the same agent | Time intervals **summed, not deduplicated** | Yes |
| Time spent in `degraded` state | Best-effort included based on last known step timestamps; if the step envelope never closed, accumulate up to the last observed event and stop | Yes |

**Pure helper** in `agentWorkingTimeServicePure.ts`:
```typescript
export function accumulateWorkingTime(
  events: AgentExecutionEvent[],
): { workingTimeSeconds: number; runCount: number; successfulRuns: number; failedRuns: number; partialRuns: number; }
```

**Reconciliation invariant.** Working Time chart total for any timeframe = the per-agent invoice line for the same timeframe. Both surfaces read from the same `agent_working_time_rollups` table. Tested via pure unit. The parent-run rollup (parent + sub-agent total) is computed at invoice-presentation time as `SUM(parent_agent_rollup, sub_agent_rollups)`; that total is an invoice surface, not a chart on the parent's Overview tab. Per-agent charts and per-agent invoice lines reconcile 1:1.

**Hover affordance.** Each chart bar surfaces the run id(s) that contributed to the bucket ƒ?" operator's escape hatch when reconciling against the invoice.

### 7.6 Home widget section ordering (brief ¶õ6)

**Pure comparator** `orderHomePresenceSections(rows)`:

Section order (top to bottom):
1. **Waiting on you** (`waiting_on_human`) ƒ?" operator action required to unblock. Top 5 visible; overflow `+N more waiting on you`.
2. **Working now** (`running`) ƒ?" Top 5 visible; overflow `+N more working`. Footer: `+M paused on system` (`waiting_on_dependency` count).
3. **Failing** (`failed`) ƒ?" Top 5 visible; overflow `+N more failing`. Section hidden when empty.
4. **Scheduled next** (`scheduled`) ƒ?" Top 5 visible; overflow `+N more scheduled today`. Sort by `next_run_at ASC` within section.
5. **Idle** (`idle`) ƒ?" NOT shown; accessed via *All agents* link.

Within each section (except *Scheduled next*): sort by `updated_at DESC`.

`waiting_on_dependency` agents are intentionally NOT a peer section ƒ?" count rolled into *Working now* footer.

`degraded` agents float into whichever section their `degraded_base_state` would have placed them; the *Status uncertain* badge surfaces the trust signal. The `agent_presence_projections.degraded_base_state` column (¶õ6.3) is the authoritative input ƒ?" pure-function ordering doesn't synthesise the section from raw signals.

**Cap.** Widget total height ƒ%Ï17 rows (5 + section header Ç- 4 + footer) regardless of agency size. Spec implementation must mock the 20-running case before declaring layout shippable.

### 7.7 Run-trace lineage chip (brief ¶õ8)

**Tuple:** `(run_id, event_id, produced_file_id, produced_version_id)`.

**Click resolution:**
- Default click: opens artifact at `produced_version_id` in Knowledge ƒÅ' Files. File chrome shows *"As produced by Outreach Agent run 1283, step 7, 2 days ago"* + `View latest` affordance.
- Chip never silently re-binds to a newer version.
- A small *Newer version available* badge MAY appear on the chip when the version is no longer current; link target stays bound.

**Layout caps:**
- Maximum visible chips per event: **4**. Beyond 4: render first 4 + `+N more` inline-expandable.
- Chronological ordering invariant: causal order (the order in which the parent event produced them). NEVER alphabetic, NEVER MIME-grouped.
- Filename truncation: **36 characters**, middle-ellipsis preserving extension.
- Maximum event-row height before overflow: **3 lines**, then `Show more` expandable.
- Detail panel (right column on Run trace) is the spillover for full content.

**Phase 1 deep-link contract** (locked in ¶õ15): `?agentId=...&runId=...&eventId=...&fileId=...&versionId=...`. Phase 1's Knowledge ƒÅ' Files tab MUST accept and resolve this query parameter.

**Cross-org leak guard for SSE.** The presence stream MUST validate `organisation_id` and `subaccount_id` on every event push; cross-org subscriptions are rejected at handshake time. `agent_presence_projections_org_isolation` policy ensures the publisher's read query already filters; the handshake check is defence-in-depth.

## 9. Execution model

Picked once per surface; the rest of the spec is consistent with the choice.

| Surface | Model | Cache / partition | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| Status pill (`AgentPresenceState`) | Server-pushed (SSE) | Read from `agent_presence_projections`; pushed on tail-event | <5s end-to-end |
| Current focus | Server-pushed alongside pill | Same channel | <5s end-to-end |
| Activity feed | Append stream over same SSE channel | None | <10s |
| Recent observations | Append stream | None ƒ?" reads `agent_observations` | <10s |
| Working Time chart (active timeframe) | Server-pushed for the bucket containing "now"; older buckets immutable | Reads `agent_working_time_rollups` | <30s |
| Working Time chart (other timeframes) | Cached read on tab-pill click | TTL 60s | Lazy-fetch |
| Knowledge in use | Event projection from Phase 1 retrieval observability | Active-run live; otherwise last-run snapshot | <5s active; immediate on run-end |
| Files snapshot | Cached per-agent slice of Phase 1 Files projection | TTL 60s | Refresh on run-end |
| Tools usage bands | Materialised aggregation | Cache 1h | Bands shift slowly |
| Connections health | Cached read | TTL 60s | Connections page is live; Overview snapshot is the cached read |
| Schedule peek | Cached read | TTL 60s | |
| Identity card | Static (read on tab mount) | None | No live updates |
| Home widget | Same SSE channel multiplexed for workspace scope | None | <5s |

**Cross-cutting rule:** surfaces driven by SSE share **one connection per Overview tab** and one connection per Home widget. No three-independent-channels pattern.

**Idempotency check:** `agent_presence_projections` upserts use `INSERT ƒ?Ý ON CONFLICT (agent_id) DO UPDATE` with the ¶õ11.1 watermark predicate (per-run `(last_event_run_id, last_event_run_seq)` plus cross-run server-side `last_event_timestamp` tiebreaker). The watermark composes per-run + cross-run because `agent_execution_events.sequence_number` is run-scoped, not global; replayed events never overwrite newer state (brief ¶õ5.2 *no rollback by replay*).

**No new service layer.** Reuse `agentExecutionEventService` for emission; reuse existing `withOrgTx` for tenant isolation. The presence projection writer is a function inside `agentPresenceService`, not a parallel pipeline.

## 10. Phase sequencing (dependency graph)

Forward-only. No phase references a primitive introduced in a later phase.

| Phase | Schema introduced | Services introduced | Services modified | Jobs introduced | Columns referenced by code |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | `agent_observations`, `iee_sessions`, `agent_presence_projections`, `agent_working_time_rollups`; columns on `iee_artifacts` | `agentPresenceService`, `agentObservationService`, `agentWorkingTimeService`, `ieeSessionService` (skeleton only ƒ?" full lifecycle in Phase 4), pure helpers | `agentExecutionEventService` | none | All Phase-1 tables, `agent_execution_events`, `agent_runs` |
| 2 | `users.default_agent_tab` | `agentOverviewAggregator`, overview-route handler | none | none | Phase-1 tables, `agent_runs`, `users.default_agent_tab` |
| 3 | none | `agentPresenceStreamPublisher` | `agentPresenceService` | none | Phase-1, Phase-2 tables |
| 4 | none | `ieeSessionService` (full implementation) | `ieeExecutionService` | `ieeSessionOrphanCleanup`, `ieeSessionsCompactJob`, `agentObservationsPruneJob`, `workingTimeRollupCompactJob` | `iee_sessions`, `iee_runs`, `iee_steps`, `iee_artifacts` |

| 6 | none | none | none | none | none ƒ?" capability docs only |

**Backward dependency check:** Phase 5 reads `iee_artifacts.producing_event_id` and `produced_version_id`, which are added in Phase 1 ƒ?" forward.
**Orphaned deferral check:** `is_pinned` column added Phase 1, surface in v1.1 (¶õ18 deferred); the column exists at v1 build time so no orphaned deferral.
**Phase-boundary contradiction check:** every phase's column references are introduced in itself or earlier; no claim of "no migrations" carries a migration in the inventory.

## 11. Execution-safety contracts

Per spec-authoring checklist Section 10, every new write path declares idempotency / retry / concurrency / terminal events.

### 11.1 Idempotency posture

| Operation | Posture | Mechanism |
|---|---|---|
| `INSERT INTO agent_observations` | `key-based` | `UNIQUE (idempotency_key)` ƒ?" duplicate observation emit for the same logical observation is rejected. The key is computed by the writer from `(event_id, source_id, observation_type, normalised_body_hash)` so multiple distinct observations of the same type from the same event are permitted. `(supersedes_observation_id)` is allowed many-to-one (multiple corrections superseding the same root). |
| `INSERT INTO iee_sessions` | `key-based` | `UNIQUE (run_id)` ƒ?" second session-creation for the same run rejected with 409 (mapped from 23505). |
| `UPSERT agent_presence_projections` | `state-based` | Predicate: accept if `(excluded.last_event_run_id = projections.last_event_run_id AND excluded.last_event_run_seq > projections.last_event_run_seq) OR excluded.last_event_timestamp > projections.last_event_timestamp`. Per-run sequence is the within-run watermark; cross-run uses server-side monotonic timestamp from `agent_execution_events.event_timestamp`. |
| `INSERT INTO agent_working_time_rollups` (upsert) | `key-based` | The ledger is the single mechanism. `agent_working_time_event_ledger.event_id` is the PK; the writer inserts into the ledger first (`INSERT INTO ledger ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING RETURNING event_id`); only on a non-empty RETURNING does it apply the contribution to the rollup bucket(s) in the same transaction. Replays, retries, and out-of-order events are all idempotent. The rollup table has no sequence watermark of its own; idempotency lives at the per-event ledger. |
| `INSERT INTO iee_artifacts` (with `producing_event_id`, `produced_version_id`) | `key-based` | `produced_version_id` is allocated at write time; subsequent re-writes of the same logical filename produce a new row with a new version id. No upsert path ƒ?" every write is a new row. |
| Session heartbeat update | `safe` (state-based) | `UPDATE ƒ?Ý WHERE id = $1 AND status IN ('active','idle')` ƒ?" heartbeat after teardown is a no-op (0 rows updated). |
| Session teardown | `guarded` | Optimistic predicate `WHERE status IN ('active','idle')`; second teardown returns the prior teardown's result (the existing `release_reason`). |

### 11.2 Retry classification

| Operation | Class | Boundary |
|---|---|---|
| Observation append | `guarded` | UNIQUE on `idempotency_key` (computed by writer from `(event_id, source_id, observation_type, normalised_body_hash)`) |
| Session create | `guarded` | UNIQUE on `run_id` |
| Presence projection upsert | `safe` | Sequence-watermark predicate |
| Working-time rollup upsert | `guarded` | `agent_working_time_event_ledger` PK on `event_id` ƒ?" replays produce 0-row ledger inserts, which short-circuit the rollup contribution |
| Heartbeat | `safe` | Idempotent; 0-rows-updated path is no-op |
| Session teardown | `guarded` | Optimistic predicate `WHERE status IN ('active','idle')` |
| Stream reconnect with `Last-Event-ID` | `safe` | Server filters events on `(event_timestamp, event_id) > (lastSeen)`; older events are recorded for audit but not re-applied to live projection |

### 11.3 Concurrency guards

| Race | Guard | Losing-caller response |
|---|---|---|
| Two parallel runs of same agent (concurrent scheduled triggers) | Two distinct `iee_sessions` rows ƒ?" `UNIQUE (run_id)` permits this. Working-time intervals **sum, not deduplicate** (brief ¶õ5.4). | n/a ƒ?" both win |
| Two writers attempting to create a session for the same run | `UNIQUE (run_id)` ƒÅ' 23505 ƒÅ' mapped to HTTP 409 with error body referencing the existing session id | 409 with `{ existingSessionId: ... }` |
| Two correctors superseding the same observation | Allowed; both `supersedes_observation_id = X` rows exist. The Overview surface displays the *latest* by `created_at`. The audit history shows both. | n/a ƒ?" both stored |
| Two clients both attempting to set the user's default tab simultaneously (v1.1 only ƒ?" no v1 write path) | Last-write-wins (`users.default_agent_tab` is a single column) | 200 with the persisted value |
| Replay storm (event stream reconnect) | Sequence-watermark on `agent_presence_projections.(last_event_run_id, last_event_run_seq)` + cross-run timestamp tiebreaker; `agent_working_time_event_ledger` makes per-event folding key-based and idempotent ƒ?" older replayed events ignored | n/a ƒ?" silently skipped, audit logged |
| Two heartbeats for same session arriving simultaneously | `UPDATE ƒ?Ý WHERE id = $1 AND status IN ('active','idle')` ƒ?" both updates succeed (last `last_heartbeat_at` wins) | n/a ƒ?" both succeed |

### 11.4 Terminal events

| Chain | Terminal event | Status field | Post-terminal prohibition |
|---|---|---|---|
| Run lifecycle (existing) | `run_completed` (existing) | `success | partial | failed` | No new events with same `run_id` after terminal ƒ?" existing contract |
| Session lifecycle | Session row's `released_at` set | `release_reason` ƒ^^ closed enum | No further state transitions; `torn_down ƒÅ' *` forbidden |
| Observation thread | Latest non-superseded row | n/a (each row is its own truth) | A superseded row never re-emerges as canonical |

**No-silent-partial-success rule.** Run terminal events that complete with partial side-effects emit `status = 'partial'`. The Overview Working Time chart accounts the run as `partial_runs += 1`; the Working Time bar is coloured indigo (success portion) with red overlay (failed portion) per the brief ¶õ5 caption rule.

### 11.5 Unique-constraint ƒÅ' HTTP mapping

| Constraint | HTTP | Body |
|---|---|---|
| `iee_sessions UNIQUE (run_id)` | 409 | `{ "error": { "code": "session_already_exists", "existingSessionId": "..." } }` |
| `agent_observations UNIQUE (idempotency_key)` | 200 (idempotent hit ƒ?" service treats the existing row as success) | Returns the existing observation row |
| `users.default_agent_tab` (v1.1 only ƒ?" no v1 write path) | 200 (idempotent ƒ?" the value is what was set) | n/a |
| `iee_artifacts UNIQUE` (existing) | n/a ƒ?" every write produces a new row with a new `produced_version_id`; no upsert path | n/a |

No 23505 ever bubbles as 500. Mapping enforced inside the service writer, not at the route boundary.

### 11.6 Working Time accounting reconciliation

Pure-function unit test: `accumulateWorkingTime(events)` for the closed-table cases in ¶õ7.5 and the brief ¶õ5.4. The reconciliation invariant ƒ?" chart total equals invoice total ƒ?" is asserted at the test level by computing both from the same `agent_working_time_rollups` rows and asserting equality. If a future invoice surface diverges (e.g. introduces its own rollup), this invariant must hold at the call-site or be explicitly broken with a recorded ADR.

### 11.7 Anti-stale clock guard (brief ¶õ5.1 hard rule, ¶õ5.3 clock authority)

The freshness thresholds form one closed set, declared as constants in `shared/types/agentPresence.ts` and used by both the projection writer and the pure tests:

```typescript
export const PRESENCE_FRESHNESS_THRESHOLDS_MS = {
  EVENT_STREAM_DELAYED:   10_000,   // ¶õ12.3 entry to `degraded` with reason 'event_stream_delayed'
  WORKER_HEARTBEAT_STALE: 30_000,   // ¶õ12.3 entry to `degraded` with reason 'worker_heartbeat_stale'
  FOCUS_LINE_STALE_COPY:  30_000,   // ¶õ5.1 stale-state copy threshold (one source-of-truth value)
  DEGRADED_HYSTERESIS:    10_000,   // ¶õ12.3 minimum dwell in degraded
  DEGRADED_OSCILLATION_WINDOW: 30_000, // ¶õ12.3 anti-oscillation window
  DEGRADED_OSCILLATION_HOLD:    60_000, // ¶õ12.3 anti-oscillation hold time
} as const;
```

`Current focus` displays MUST be wrapped in a freshness check at the resolver level: if the latest event's age exceeds `EVENT_STREAM_DELAYED` (10s) while status = `running`, the projection writer transitions `presence_state` to `degraded` with `degraded_reason = 'event_stream_delayed'` (per ¶õ12.3). The focus line is replaced with the ¶õ5.1 stale-state copy when the age exceeds `FOCUS_LINE_STALE_COPY` (30s). Both thresholds are enforced at projection-write time, not at the client.

`failed` is reserved for terminal failure events emitted by the run engine ƒ?" never inferred from telemetry silence. If the run truly completed while telemetry was stale, the next received event resolves `degraded` to `idle` per ¶õ12.3 *State on resolution*. If the run is genuinely stuck (no terminal event ever arrives), the agent stays in `degraded` until the worker heartbeat times out, at which point the orphan-cleanup path (Phase 4) writes a terminal failure event and the projection transitions to `failed` via the canonical chain.

---

## 12. State machine ƒ?" `AgentPresenceState`

### 12.1 Closed status set

Seven values: `idle | running | waiting_on_human | waiting_on_dependency | scheduled | degraded | failed`. Adding a new value requires a spec amendment (¶õ7.1 enforcement). The Postgres `CHECK` constraint on `agent_presence_projections.presence_state` is the database-level enforcement; the TypeScript discriminated union is the application-level enforcement.

### 12.2 Valid transitions

```
idle ƒÅ" running
idle ƒÅ" scheduled
idle ƒÅ" degraded
running ƒÅ" waiting_on_human
running ƒÅ" waiting_on_dependency
running ƒÅ" degraded
running ƒÅ' idle (run completed cleanly)
running ƒÅ' failed
waiting_on_human ƒÅ' running (operator unblocks)
waiting_on_human ƒÅ' failed (operator rejects / timeout)
waiting_on_dependency ƒÅ' running (dependency resolves)
waiting_on_dependency ƒÅ' failed (dependency permanently unavailable)
waiting_on_dependency ƒÅ' degraded (telemetry uncertain)
scheduled ƒÅ' running (scheduled time arrives)
scheduled ƒÅ' idle (run cancelled before fire)
degraded ƒÅ' <freshly resolved primary state> (per ¶õ12.3 ƒ?" resolver re-runs the ¶õ7.1 chain; NOT a return to the pre-degradation state)
failed ƒÅ' idle (operator acknowledges; manual recovery)
```

**Forbidden:** any transition not listed. `failed ƒÅ' running` directly is forbidden ƒ?" the agent must transition through `idle` (operator-acknowledged recovery). Forbidden transitions are caught at the projection-writer layer; the writer rejects an upsert that would produce an illegal transition and logs `presence.illegal_transition_attempt` for audit.

### 12.3 `degraded` recovery semantics (brief ¶õ5.2)

Entry conditions (any one is sufficient):

| Condition | Detection | UI subtitle |
|---|---|---|
| `event_stream_delayed` | Server detects no new event from this run for 10s while activity is expected | Subtitle: "Presence delayedƒ?Ý" |
| `worker_heartbeat_stale` | The IEE worker handling this run has not pinged in 30s | Subtitle: "Status uncertain" |
| `focus_source_unavailable` | The latest event has no summarisable content | "(focus snapshot, X seconds ago)" |

These three **server-observed** conditions are the only ones that populate `agent_presence_projections.degraded_reason`; the table's CHECK constraint pins the closed list. Each is detected on the server and is shared truth across all surfaces.

**Client-side transport failures are NOT canonical presence.** When the client's SSE connection drops (network blip, tab paused, load-balancer flap), the client renders a **local** banner ("Reconnectingƒ?Ý") and freezes its tickers. The server-side `agent_presence_projections.presence_state` is unchanged ƒ?" every other surface viewing the same agent continues to see the live state. Local transport health and canonical presence are two separate signals; conflating them lets one tab's disconnect mutate global state, which violates the brief ¶õ5.3 single-source-of-truth invariant. This separation is hard.

**Recovery threshold.** `degraded` clears only after **two consecutive healthy heartbeat intervals** observed by the server-side projection writer. Recovery is entirely server-observed. Client-side resync acknowledgements (when an SSE client reconnects with `Last-Event-ID`) are a separate non-canonical signal that affects only that client's local UI; they do NOT mutate `agent_presence_projections.presence_state` (per the ¶õ12.3 client-vs-canonical separation).

**Hysteresis window.** Minimum **10 seconds** in `degraded` before transitioning back. Prevents one-packet flicker. Implemented at the projection writer ƒ?" the writer rejects a `degraded ƒÅ' primary` upsert if `NOW() - degraded_entered_at < INTERVAL '10 seconds'`.

**Anti-oscillation rule.** If `degraded ƒÅ' healthy ƒÅ' degraded` happens twice within a 30-second window, the agent stays in `degraded` for the full 60-second hysteresis period regardless of subsequent healthy heartbeats. `degraded_oscillation_count` field on `agent_presence_projections` tracks within-window count; reset by the projection writer when the 30-second window elapses without an oscillation.

**State on resolution.** Transitions to whatever the primary state actually is ƒ?" derived fresh from the ¶õ7.1 resolution chain ƒ?" not back to whatever it was before the degradation began. If the agent finished its run while telemetry was degraded, the resolved state is `idle`, not the prior `running`.

### 12.4 Replay semantics (brief ¶õ5.2 hard rule)

- Events apply strictly in `(event_timestamp, event_id)` order.
- Duplicate events (same `event_id`) detected and ignored on second arrival.
- **Older replayed events never overwrite newer resolved state.** If a replayed event's `event_timestamp = T1` arrives after the projection has advanced past `T2 > T1`, the event is recorded for audit but is NOT re-applied to the live presence projection.
- Out-of-order arrival within a batch is fine; the projection sorts before applying.

This is enforced at the projection upsert layer (¶õ11.1 sequence-watermark predicate).

602:### 6.5 Run-trace produced-file lineage (Phase 1, migration 0288 — extension to `iee_artifacts`)
604:The brief requires every chip to resolve on `(run_id, event_id, produced_file_id, produced_version_id)`. The existing `iee_artifacts` table is keyed on `iee_run_id` (FK to `iee_runs.id`), not directly on `agent_runs.id`. The join path from agent run → artifact is `agent_runs.id → agent_runs.iee_run_id (= iee_runs.id) → iee_artifacts.iee_run_id`. We extend the table with:
608:  ADD COLUMN agent_run_id UUID REFERENCES agent_runs(id),               -- denormalised for lineage queries; populated at write time
612:CREATE INDEX iee_artifacts_agent_run_idx ON iee_artifacts (agent_run_id) WHERE agent_run_id IS NOT NULL;
617:The lineage four-tuple is therefore `(agent_run_id, producing_event_id, id, produced_version_id)`. The Phase 1 deep-link query parameter shape (§15.1) maps `runId → agent_run_id`, `eventId → producing_event_id`, `fileId → iee_artifacts.id`, `versionId → produced_version_id`.
619:`produced_version_id` is allocated at the moment the artifact is written; subsequent re-writes of the same logical filename produce a *new* row with a new `produced_version_id`. Every chip is keyed on the four-tuple; clicks resolve to the exact version produced at that event.
621:**Backfill:** `agent_run_id` is nullable for legacy rows. New writes set it; existing rows stay null. Phase 5 chips render only for events whose `iee_artifacts` rows have all four fields populated; legacy rows surface as un-chipped events with no degradation in the surrounding UI.
628:    CHECK (default_agent_tab IN ('overview','configure','behaviour','personality','skills','scorecards','data-sources','schedule','budget','runs'));
631:Per-user preference; the AgentEditPage reads it on mount. No feature flag. New column only; no backfill required (`DEFAULT 'overview'` covers existing rows).
635:| Class | Source | Retention | Pruning job |
637:| Run lifecycle events (canonical) | `agent_execution_events` | Indefinite | None — immutable. |
638:| Typed observations | `agent_observations` | 90 days default; `is_pinned = TRUE` indefinite | `agentObservationsPruneJob` daily. |
639:| Retrieval summaries | `retrieval.summary` events | Owned by Phase 1 — 30 days at full fidelity | Phase 1 owns. |
640:| Current focus snapshots | In-memory (Redis or equivalent) | Ephemeral, session-bound | TTL 60s on each cache write. Never persisted. |
642:| Session summaries | `iee_sessions.summary` | 90 days | `ieeSessionsCompactJob` daily — compacts blobs older than 90d, retains row. |
645:Pruning a projection MUST NOT invalidate any user-visible surface; if Overview surfaces data older than the retention window, the surface fails closed (shows *"older than X days, view in Run trace"*) rather than rendering stale data.
659:  'running',
673:2. degraded            — any §12.3 degradation condition is currently true AND no terminal event present
674:3. waiting_on_human    — active run is paused at a HITL gate
675:4. running             — active run has at least one step in flight
676:5. waiting_on_dependency — active run is paused on external system / lock / retry / sub-agent
677:6. scheduled           — no active run, next run time is known
681:`failed` ranks above `degraded` because telemetry staleness must never mask a canonical terminal failure. If the run has emitted a terminal failure event, the resolver returns `failed` regardless of the freshness of subsequent telemetry. `degraded` is only entered when the run is still in flight per the canonical event log AND telemetry has gone stale.
684:**Consumers:** every presence-aware UI surface (Overview hero pill, Home Active Agents widget, sidebar agent list, run trace header, activity badges, Inbox notifications) reads from this projection. UI MUST NOT re-derive state from raw signals (brief §5.3).
688:### 7.2 `CurrentFocus`
694:export interface CurrentFocus {
696:  truncated: boolean;
700:    | 'active_run_step'
702:    | 'scheduled_next_run'
703:    | 'last_completed_run'
704:    | 'static_fallback';
711:1. `agent_runs.current_step_summary` of the active run (latest non-idle step).
713:3. `scheduled_next_run` description, when status = `scheduled`.
714:4. `last_completed_run.summary`, when status = `idle`.
715:5. Static fallback per brief §5.1 stale-state copy ("No recent activity (last event 4m ago)" with the actual age).
717:**Anti-fake-progress validator** (brief §5.1 hard rule): the focus-line summariser rejects copy that lacks at least one of (a) a concrete step number, (b) a concrete entity / object id or name, or (c) a concrete blocking condition. Forbidden patterns: `*Thinking*`, `*Analysing data*`, `*Working on task*`, `*Reasoning about*`, `*Preparing*`, `*Processing*`, any `-ing` verb without an object. If the latest event has no concrete subject, the focus line falls back to the explicit stale-state copy rather than synthesising filler.
719:**Producer:** `agentPresenceService` (server-side, runs at projection-update time).
722:Truncation: 140 characters before middle-ellipsis on desktop; tighter on narrower viewports per existing responsive pattern.
731:**Provenance invariant:** every row has `event_id` set. `event_id` references `agent_execution_events.id` for run-derived observations (`learned`, `detected`, `decided`, `flagged`, `produced`). The row's `metadata.source_kind` field discriminates the origin (closed enum: `run_step | retrieval_summary | tool_result | memory_block_insert`); the `metadata.source_id` field carries the underlying entity id (e.g. `agent_execution_events.id`, retrieval-summary event id, structured tool result id, `memory_blocks.id`).
733:**Append-only invariant:** there is no `UPDATE` path. Corrections create a new row with `supersedes_observation_id` set. The Overview surface reads the latest non-superseded row in each thread; the run trace and audit views show the full history.
741:  "run_id": "run...",
746:    "source_kind": "run_step",
756:**Producer:** `agentObservationService.append(...)` invoked from the run-step terminal-event hook in `agentExecutionService` and from the retrieval-summary handler.
768:    "state": "running",
770:    "activeRunId": "run...",
771:    "currentFocus": { /* CurrentFocus */ },
772:    "elapsedSinceRunStartMs": 14211,
775:  "activeGoals": [ { "type": "scheduled_run", "label": "Weekly Acme outreach", "nextRunAt": "..." } ],
785:  "schedulePeek": { "nextRunAt": "...", "trigger": "weekly_cron", "label": "Weekly Acme outreach" },
791:    "captionRunsCount": 0,
793:    "captionAverageRunDurationSeconds": 0
808:**Inline-content prohibition** (brief §5.8): activity-feed rows reference `event_id` only; full event content fetched on click. Recent-observation rows beyond the initial 3 reference `observation_id` only. Knowledge-in-use entries hold metadata + source-document id; never embed source text inline. Run-trace lineage chips reference the four-tuple only.
810:**Worst-case profiling:** spec author MUST profile the *50-runs-today, 200-pinned-observations, 30-knowledge-entries-loaded* worst case before declaring layout shippable. The 150KB target holds at the 95th-percentile worst case; design for graceful degradation (more aggressive lazy-loading) above it rather than blowing the budget.
816:**Definition:** Working Time is the sum of intervals during which an `agent_execution_events.step_started` event has fired and a matching `step_completed` event has not yet fired, for runs owned by this agent — **minus** any nested intervals where the worker is in a declared wait state (HITL pause, external dependency wait, retry backoff). The accounting boundary is *worker-side compute*: the run engine and the IEE worker emit explicit start/end events when entering and exiting wait states; Working Time accumulates only outside those wait windows.
826:| `retry_backoff_started` → `retry_backoff_completed` | **Subtracted** | Worker is sleeping. |
829:**Inclusion / exclusion summary:**
833:| Active LLM call or worker-local tool call (state = `running`, no nested wait state) | Yes | Yes |
837:| Retry backoff between attempts | No | No |
838:| Sub-agent delegation | Yes for parent (only for non-delegated portions) and Yes for sub-agent (both attributed separately; rolls up to parent run for invoice) | Yes for both |
840:| Concurrent runs of the same agent | Time intervals **summed, not deduplicated** | Yes |
847:): { workingTimeSeconds: number; runCount: number; successfulRuns: number; failedRuns: number; partialRuns: number; }
850:**Reconciliation invariant.** Working Time chart total for any timeframe = the per-agent invoice line for the same timeframe. Both surfaces read from the same `agent_working_time_rollups` table. Tested via pure unit. The parent-run rollup (parent + sub-agent total) is computed at invoice-presentation time as `SUM(parent_agent_rollup, sub_agent_rollups)`; that total is an invoice surface, not a chart on the parent's Overview tab. Per-agent charts and per-agent invoice lines reconcile 1:1.
852:**Hover affordance.** Each chart bar surfaces the run id(s) that contributed to the bucket — operator's escape hatch when reconciling against the invoice.
860:2. **Working now** (`running`) — Top 5 visible; overflow `+N more working`. Footer: `+M paused on system` (`waiting_on_dependency` count).
862:4. **Scheduled next** (`scheduled`) — Top 5 visible; overflow `+N more scheduled today`. Sort by `next_run_at ASC` within section.
871:**Cap.** Widget total height ≤17 rows (5 + section header × 4 + footer) regardless of agency size. Spec implementation must mock the 20-running case before declaring layout shippable.

943:**Idempotency check:** `agent_presence_projections` upserts use `INSERT … ON CONFLICT (agent_id) DO UPDATE` with the §11.1 watermark predicate (per-run `(last_event_run_id, last_event_run_seq)` plus cross-run server-side `last_event_timestamp` tiebreaker). The watermark composes per-run + cross-run because `agent_execution_events.sequence_number` is run-scoped, not global; replayed events never overwrite newer state (brief §5.2 *no rollback by replay*).
955:| 1 | `agent_observations`, `iee_sessions`, `agent_presence_projections`, `agent_working_time_rollups`; columns on `iee_artifacts` | `agentPresenceService`, `agentObservationService`, `agentWorkingTimeService`, `ieeSessionService` (skeleton only — full lifecycle in Phase 4), pure helpers | `agentExecutionEventService` | none | All Phase-1 tables, `agent_execution_events`, `agent_runs` |

962:**Backward dependency check:** Phase 5 reads `iee_artifacts.producing_event_id` and `produced_version_id`, which are added in Phase 1 — forward.
977:| `INSERT INTO iee_sessions` | `key-based` | `UNIQUE (run_id)` — second session-creation for the same run rejected with 409 (mapped from 23505). |
978:| `UPSERT agent_presence_projections` | `state-based` | Predicate: accept if `(excluded.last_event_run_id = projections.last_event_run_id AND excluded.last_event_run_seq > projections.last_event_run_seq) OR excluded.last_event_timestamp > projections.last_event_timestamp`. Per-run sequence is the within-run watermark; cross-run uses server-side monotonic timestamp from `agent_execution_events.event_timestamp`. |
989:| Session create | `guarded` | UNIQUE on `run_id` |
994:| Stream reconnect with `Last-Event-ID` | `safe` | Server filters events on `(event_timestamp, event_id) > (lastSeen)`; older events are recorded for audit but not re-applied to live projection |
1000:| Two parallel runs of same agent (concurrent scheduled triggers) | Two distinct `iee_sessions` rows — `UNIQUE (run_id)` permits this. Working-time intervals **sum, not deduplicate** (brief §5.4). | n/a — both win |
1001:| Two writers attempting to create a session for the same run | `UNIQUE (run_id)` → 23505 → mapped to HTTP 409 with error body referencing the existing session id | 409 with `{ existingSessionId: ... }` |
1002:| Two correctors superseding the same observation | Allowed; both `supersedes_observation_id = X` rows exist. The Overview surface displays the *latest* by `created_at`. The audit history shows both. | n/a — both stored |
1004:| Replay storm (event stream reconnect) | Sequence-watermark on `agent_presence_projections.(last_event_run_id, last_event_run_seq)` + cross-run timestamp tiebreaker; `agent_working_time_event_ledger` makes per-event folding key-based and idempotent — older replayed events ignored | n/a — silently skipped, audit logged |
1011:| Run lifecycle (existing) | `run_completed` (existing) | `success | partial | failed` | No new events with same `run_id` after terminal — existing contract |
1013:| Observation thread | Latest non-superseded row | n/a (each row is its own truth) | A superseded row never re-emerges as canonical |
1015:**No-silent-partial-success rule.** Run terminal events that complete with partial side-effects emit `status = 'partial'`. The Overview Working Time chart accounts the run as `partial_runs += 1`; the Working Time bar is coloured indigo (success portion) with red overlay (failed portion) per the brief §5 caption rule.
1021:| `iee_sessions UNIQUE (run_id)` | 409 | `{ "error": { "code": "session_already_exists", "existingSessionId": "..." } }` |
1030:Pure-function unit test: `accumulateWorkingTime(events)` for the closed-table cases in §7.5 and the brief §5.4. The reconciliation invariant — chart total equals invoice total — is asserted at the test level by computing both from the same `agent_working_time_rollups` rows and asserting equality. If a future invoice surface diverges (e.g. introduces its own rollup), this invariant must hold at the call-site or be explicitly broken with a recorded ADR.
1040:  FOCUS_LINE_STALE_COPY:  30_000,   // §5.1 stale-state copy threshold (one source-of-truth value)
1047:`Current focus` displays MUST be wrapped in a freshness check at the resolver level: if the latest event's age exceeds `EVENT_STREAM_DELAYED` (10s) while status = `running`, the projection writer transitions `presence_state` to `degraded` with `degraded_reason = 'event_stream_delayed'` (per §12.3). The focus line is replaced with the §5.1 stale-state copy when the age exceeds `FOCUS_LINE_STALE_COPY` (30s). Both thresholds are enforced at projection-write time, not at the client.
1049:`failed` is reserved for terminal failure events emitted by the run engine — never inferred from telemetry silence. If the run truly completed while telemetry was stale, the next received event resolves `degraded` to `idle` per §12.3 *State on resolution*. If the run is genuinely stuck (no terminal event ever arrives), the agent stays in `degraded` until the worker heartbeat times out, at which point the orphan-cleanup path (Phase 4) writes a terminal failure event and the projection transitions to `failed` via the canonical chain.
1057:Seven values: `idle | running | waiting_on_human | waiting_on_dependency | scheduled | degraded | failed`. Adding a new value requires a spec amendment (§7.1 enforcement). The Postgres `CHECK` constraint on `agent_presence_projections.presence_state` is the database-level enforcement; the TypeScript discriminated union is the application-level enforcement.
1062:idle ↔ running
1065:running ↔ waiting_on_human
1066:running ↔ waiting_on_dependency
1067:running ↔ degraded
1068:running → idle (run completed cleanly)
1069:running → failed
1070:waiting_on_human → running (operator unblocks)
1072:waiting_on_dependency → running (dependency resolves)
1075:scheduled → running (scheduled time arrives)
1076:scheduled → idle (run cancelled before fire)
1077:degraded → <freshly resolved primary state> (per §12.3 — resolver re-runs the §7.1 chain; NOT a return to the pre-degradation state)
1081:**Forbidden:** any transition not listed. `failed → running` directly is forbidden — the agent must transition through `idle` (operator-acknowledged recovery). Forbidden transitions are caught at the projection-writer layer; the writer rejects an upsert that would produce an illegal transition and logs `presence.illegal_transition_attempt` for audit.
1089:| `event_stream_delayed` | Server detects no new event from this run for 10s while activity is expected | Subtitle: "Presence delayed…" |
1090:| `worker_heartbeat_stale` | The IEE worker handling this run has not pinged in 30s | Subtitle: "Status uncertain" |
1091:| `focus_source_unavailable` | The latest event has no summarisable content | "(focus snapshot, X seconds ago)" |
1099:**Hysteresis window.** Minimum **10 seconds** in `degraded` before transitioning back. Prevents one-packet flicker. Implemented at the projection writer — the writer rejects a `degraded → primary` upsert if `NOW() - degraded_entered_at < INTERVAL '10 seconds'`.
1103:**State on resolution.** Transitions to whatever the primary state actually is — derived fresh from the §7.1 resolution chain — not back to whatever it was before the degradation began. If the agent finished its run while telemetry was degraded, the resolved state is `idle`, not the prior `running`.
1109:- **Older replayed events never overwrite newer resolved state.** If a replayed event's `event_timestamp = T1` arrives after the projection has advanced past `T2 > T1`, the event is recorded for audit but is NOT re-applied to the live presence projection.
1135:Every event carries a server-emitted `id:` line (which the browser's `EventSource` automatically tracks as `lastEventId` for reconnect). The `id:` value is the `agent_execution_events.id` UUID for run-derived events, or a server-allocated UUID for transport-layer events (heartbeat, presence-projection-only updates).
1143:event: current_focus_updated
1144:data: { agentId, focus: CurrentFocus }
1156:data: { agentId, bucketDate, workingTimeSeconds, runCounts }
1165:- The browser's native `EventSource` automatically sends `Last-Event-ID: <last-seen-id>` as a header on reconnect once the connection has emitted at least one `id:` line. **Initial-open** does not carry a header. To resume after a deliberate close (e.g. tab restored from background), the client passes a `lastEventId` query parameter (`GET /api/agent-presence/stream/:agentId?lastEventId=<uuid>`) on initial open; the server prefers the query param, falls back to the header, and falls back to "no resume" if neither is present.
1167:- If the client has been gone for longer than the server-side buffer (default 60s), the server sends a `presence_state_changed` event for the current canonical state (the client snaps to it) — no incremental replay. The buffer-overflow path is logged so operators can detect chronic flapping.
1180:- **Allowed local synthesis** (presentation only): animating elapsed-time counter between server updates (the *0:42 elapsed* tick is fine; underlying timestamp is server-derived); smoothing the chart bar containing "now" between aggregation pushes; local hover/focus/expand UI state.
1181:- **Forbidden synthesis** (state simulation): pre-committing presence transitions; speculative `waiting_on_human` / `failed` / `degraded` / `completed` assertions; appending observations or knowledge-in-use entries without the server event; inventing activity-feed rows; "Run started" / "Run completed" surfacing before the server-side run-lifecycle event lands.

602:### 6.5 Run-trace produced-file lineage (Phase 1, migration 0288 — extension to `iee_artifacts`)
604:The brief requires every chip to resolve on `(run_id, event_id, produced_file_id, produced_version_id)`. The existing `iee_artifacts` table is keyed on `iee_run_id` (FK to `iee_runs.id`), not directly on `agent_runs.id`. The join path from agent run → artifact is `agent_runs.id → agent_runs.iee_run_id (= iee_runs.id) → iee_artifacts.iee_run_id`. We extend the table with:
608:  ADD COLUMN agent_run_id UUID REFERENCES agent_runs(id),               -- denormalised for lineage queries; populated at write time
612:CREATE INDEX iee_artifacts_agent_run_idx ON iee_artifacts (agent_run_id) WHERE agent_run_id IS NOT NULL;
617:The lineage four-tuple is therefore `(agent_run_id, producing_event_id, id, produced_version_id)`. The Phase 1 deep-link query parameter shape (§15.1) maps `runId → agent_run_id`, `eventId → producing_event_id`, `fileId → iee_artifacts.id`, `versionId → produced_version_id`.
621:**Backfill:** `agent_run_id` is nullable for legacy rows. New writes set it; existing rows stay null. Phase 5 chips render only for events whose `iee_artifacts` rows have all four fields populated; legacy rows surface as un-chipped events with no degradation in the surrounding UI.
628:    CHECK (default_agent_tab IN ('overview','configure','behaviour','personality','skills','scorecards','data-sources','schedule','budget','runs'));

637:| Run lifecycle events (canonical) | `agent_execution_events` | Indefinite | None — immutable. |
638:| Typed observations | `agent_observations` | 90 days default; `is_pinned = TRUE` indefinite | `agentObservationsPruneJob` daily. |
